The Wozao Beach Residence 233

— Lu Heqin

A solitary thatched hut stands on the river island, daring to compare itself to Duke Wen encountering Jizhou. When successful, the blue clouds let loose and carefree, but when heartbroken by the sorrow of rain, one loses restraint. Poetry and books are useful and should be hidden in the walls, Heaven and Earth have not turned around, so bear entering the boat. The most beautiful thing is that the flowers are still blooming throughout the yard, and the tall paulownia trees above the well have already sensed the coming of autumn.

··············

Riding a thin horse alone, I return to my thatched eaves, filled with ten thousand signatures of blue silk. A withered beard scratches the remnants of the changing dynasty, and a long hoe loads the old snow and frost. Tribulus thorns have long困杨亿, The wind and moon will eventually be with Xie Qian. Ten acres of gray smoke is enough for life, and the tribute should not reach the poor alleys. I quickly put away half a lifetime of splendor and enjoyment, and unveiling my traces turns to purity and seclusion. Opening the window to draw the earth allows me to wave my sleeves, and scattering my hair tomorrow I want to play on a boat. A single pole of drizzle resembles the Pu River, and a short wall three feet high is the Tuqiu. Who is holding the mirror with white hair? Shaming the adventures of those years.

··········

I once built a cottage next to Shanglin, but now I am surprised to have fallen into the wild marshes. The wind and rain shake the bed, and my body is like a寄, The beacon fire dazzles the eyes, and the invaders are already deep. Poetry and fu, the tears of guests at Jiangguan, orchids and iris, the heart of exiled officials by the Ze River. A lead knife has not yet been cut, and my years are declining, and I cannot suppress the angry tide for long.

Virginity and Chastity 234

— Xian

Dear Friend:

When I received your gift, even though it was already the third day after our marriage, I still sincerely thank you for being so thoughtful. These many exquisite gifts, in the eyes of inland people, are probably as valuable as gold, silver, and jewels. My wife also exclaimed happily, and it took her three hours to arrange them properly. At that time, my mood was certainly different from when I am writing this letter.

Going to the National Crisis Together 235

We have been friends for three or four years, and now we have become husband and wife, so our personalities, interests, and ambitions should be familiar. After living together, just as you said, the joy in one room is harmonious. But an unexpected tragedy? Shattered my beautiful dream 丨 My wife has lost her virginity. Dear friend, don't laugh at me for being pedantic. In this day and age, talking about virginity seems too outdated. But under certain circumstances, virginity is still virginity. We have had three or four years of friendship, and in the course of those three or four years, love has proceeded openly. Originally, in a state of love, there should be no consciousness of concealment or deception. My wife has loved me passionately for three or four years, and I have loved her, but she did not tell me about this. After I discovered it, she even made all sorts of excuses, obviously wanting to shift this unfounded responsibility onto my shoulders. Dear friend, not

Page 20

to say cynical words, but if she had explained it earlier, I would not have ruined the love we had built up over three or four years. Love should be open, and she has given me too much disappointment 丨 Since arguing about this matter, the fun and passion of our honeymoon have become as cold as ice. Whether we can restore the blessing of harmonious joy in one room in the future will at least include some element of bitter laughter. Love is open, my friend. I based the virginity issue on this point and brought it up under these circumstances.

Now, let's put aside our private affairs and move on to say that chastity is the responsibility of both men and women 丨 Whether it be in morality or love, to preserve it on average. In my nearly thirty years of life, I have not lost my chastity: I am a man (excuse me for saying a traditional concept), and in an environment where it is relatively easy to lose chastity, I have not abandoned myself and violated it. But women lightly sell their chastity, which is painful to say 丨 Furthermore, if men and women are violated and coerced into losing their chastity, the law has considerable protection rights. But in the process of love, it should be open.

Now I am trying hard not to let this matter be a bone of contention between us husband and wife. Spring has already come, and if you are interested, come and play in these mountains for a few days. It would be even better if your wife could come with you. Having a few more companions to travel the mountains can make the joy in the mountains harmonious, right?

Frozen Bones 236

— Quality

A Scene from Beggar Life

["Ahua, damn it,"] a man of about forty, draped with a piece of burlap on his upper body and wearing dark, single-layered trousers, cursed anxiously towards a group of people who looked just like him: ["Tonight, we're going to die here,"].

The whistling of the wind from the power lines and the chattering of their teeth played in unison like a painful lament. The old man's groans seemed to have attracted the attention of the crowd. ["Uncle Bing, good, let's stack ourselves like last night."] The young Ahua, seemingly worldly-wise, forced a smile and answered his uncle; at the same time, he looked at the crowd, hoping they would agree with his suggestion.

White snowflakes fell from the dark sky. The usually dim streetlights were now showing their ability. A pile of pale-faced people sat and lay in front of a tall building. Their clothes were mostly different, but they were all shivering.

["Oh, I don't want to stack again."] Old Bing sighed slightly and then said: ["You young people can take it, but I haven't slept for two nights... Oh! Heaven... I wonder how many days are left."] The chattering of his teeth blurred his words.

["Old Bing, I think some big bosses will come to save us."] A middle-aged man with unusually long, dishevelled hair and a face covered in mud sat up, brushing the snow off his body with one hand and clenching his teeth hard to comfort Old Bing. ["We will have good luck one day..."]

["Old Bing, are you cold? I'll give you this."] Another young man with bright eyes and gnashing teeth took off his coat and threw it at Old Bing. He seemed to be protesting against fate. ["Damn it, I'm not convinced!"]

["Little Dog Wang, thank you, what about yourself!"] ["I must go to the company tomorrow, no matter what."] Little Dog Wang continued to speak angrily: ["No, weren't you afraid today? When you saw the foreigners..."] Ahua asked haltingly: ["Kid, I'm not afraid of heaven or earth. Their cars haven't come out these past few days."]

["In that case, we have no hope of getting in. We deserve to freeze to death!"] The middle-aged man said angrily and resentfully. After a few minutes of tension, the feeling of disappointment began to ease again. Old Bing stopped groaning. He had curled up into a ball. Little Dog Wang and Ahua were excitedly playing on the snow-covered virgin ground, even though the snowflakes were falling even harder.

...Wild pheasant rides in a chartered car, pretending to be a concubine...

...I was originally in Wolonggang...

× × × × ×

The heavy dung cart began to talk to the snow. The rustling footsteps woke Ahua from his dream. He rubbed his eyes, reached out, and pinched Little Dog Wang's nose. ["Little..."] Dog Wang, Little Dog Wang, you still want to tell stories at night, what..."]

["Bah! You harmful thing."] Little Dog Wang turned over and fell asleep again.

["Sigh! A life is not even as good as a dog's, how cold!"] Ahua cursed at the sky for a while and then lay down on the ground.

["Mama, I want food..."]

["Sir, I'm freezing to death, starving to death."]

The muddled words woke the middle-aged man with particularly long hair. When he sat up, he found that the back of his head was completely soaked in a pile of white liquid. Before curiosity could arise, overwhelming fear had conquered him. He couldn't help but crawl to Ahua's side.

["Ahua! Ahua! Your uncle is not well!"] ["What, did the foreigners catch him?"] The fierce cry caused him to ask an involuntary question, half-awake and confused.

["No, he's dead, his body is not warm anymore!"]

["What? What?"] Ahua hurriedly and frantically pushed his uncle Old Bing's body.

Soon, a large crowd of sorrowful spectators gathered in front of the door where death had arrived the night before.

The next day, a news item was published in the newspaper:

["Due to the heavy snowfall and sudden cold weather in recent days, the temperature is below zero degrees. The number of beggars who freeze to death every day has broken past records. Last night, one person also froze to death in front of the ××× Road ×× Mansion. The scene was terrible. It is heard that a philanthropist, etc., has initiated a poor people's relief center to benefit these people..."]

Another victim of the times.

Before the Engagement 237

— Sheng Hong

Plums are falling, seven of them are left! Let the gentlemen seek me, while the day is auspicious! Plums are falling, three of them are left! Let the gentlemen seek me, while today lasts! Plums are falling, let baskets be filled; let the gentlemen seek me, while they tell me so! Three Chapters on Falling Plums.

Elementary school students want to marry middle school students, middle school students want to marry college students, college students want to marry students studying abroad, and students studying abroad want to marry Ph.D.s. Our Miss Xiang is no exception. Miss Xiang is a middle school student and, of course, is qualified to marry a college student. Recently, Miss Xiang met Mr. C, a graduate of ×× University. In less than two or three days, they had a meeting, either playing mahjong or going to the cinema. This mahjong and cinema seemed to be the steps they were taking towards engagement. Before they met, their siblings-in-law worked hard to mediate, with the feeling that ["The engagement has not yet succeeded, and mediation is still needed."]. The first step was to use the cinema to get them acquainted. It would not be too late to get engaged after the fruit was ripe. That day, Mr. C invited Miss Xiang and her siblings-in-law to watch Laurel and Hardy's "Old Soldiers" at the R cinema. Miss Xiang dressed up with particular effort that day, especially on her eyebrows, as the poem says:

Cleverly drawn eyebrows, delicate and charming,

Her makeup is not yet complete, resembling a Jiang Pavilion in the morning,

Distant mountains are brushed with emerald green, palace curtains are rolled up in the evening,

Her eyes are like horizontal hooks, she finds the ink too dark, and the powder too pale,

Zhang Lang, the calligrapher, is no longer free, weary of spring, she is too weak to frown,

Instead, she makes a charming gesture.

Filling in the eyebrows cannot satisfy her autumnal longing,

Knowing that there is so much sorrow in the world, remembering fish-shaped letter seals,

Stealing glances behind her back, arranging jade hairpins together, gently moving her fingers,

Some have already taken the lead, long frowns are difficult to imitate,

Light yellow willow leaves are still there today, locked with double tips,

Trying to look in the mirror and admire herself, she is still charming.

The next day, Miss Xiang's siblings-in-law held a special banquet to treat Mr. C, and then played mahjong. A few days later, they went to the cinema again. Like this, playing mahjong today and going to the cinema tomorrow, the auspicious day for their engagement was, of course, not far away.

Ah, so mahjong and the cinema have such wonderful uses.

A Prisoner Hidden in a Rat's Nest 238

— Jing Wu

I haven't seen my old friend Mr. Cheng for two years since he began serving in the capital! Recently, he returned home on business and suddenly paid me a visit the day before yesterday. Because we had been separated for so long, I couldn't help but prepare a feast to entertain him and show my hospitality. After drinking to our heart's content, we talked about current affairs and then drifted to strange stories to add to the merriment.

I then mentioned the article "Rat's Revenge" published in this magazine last year, saying that it was extremely rare and worthy of the word "strange story!"

He said: ["Speaking of 'Rat's Revenge,' I am also reminded of a story about rats: and its degree of strangeness really surpasses 'Rat's Revenge!' Furthermore, I had also seen the article 'Rat's Revenge' at the time, thinking that it was nothing more than the author using a fable to satirize the world, in order to encourage the people of the country, and to advise future generations! Who would have known that after a few days, the news of 'A Prisoner Hidden in a Rat's Nest' would be discovered in my neighbor's house in the new capital and witnessed by me. Therefore, the things in the world cannot be affirmed as impossible simply because they have not been seen! Next door to my lodgings was a shop that sold both southern goods and meat. Last year, the money counter in the meat shop was damaged by a foot, and someone was hired to repair it. As soon as it was moved, we saw the ground covered in mounds of mud, like an ant hill, with a hole the size of a bowl beside it. When we looked into it, it was very dark. When we probed it with a bamboo pole, we immediately heard a squeaking sound. We opened the hole and saw a huge rat, fat and healthy beyond compare, with bright eyes, not afraid of people at all, raising its head, wagging its tail, and standing still. After a closer examination, we realized where this rat came from. It turned out that half a year ago, an employee named X in the southern goods shop had caught a rat and, because it was so large, jokingly nailed its four feet to a piece of wood, making it into a specimen, and placed it on the counter as a joke. Unexpectedly, it disappeared overnight, and we assumed that it had undoubtedly ended up in a cat's belly! Who would have known that its own kind would rescue it, hide it in a hole, and provide it with long-term sustenance, so that it could prolong its life and remain safe for a long time. From this, it seems that it is not only full of revenge towards other species, but also full of love for its own kind!"]

After listening to his words, I couldn't help but feel moved. Even such a small creature actually knows to love its own kind, regardless of its own difficulties, and tries its best to rescue them! Compared to some warlords, who either do not resist when they are attacked by bandits, or turn their weapons against each other and destroy each other; who turn a blind eye to the compatriots who have fallen into the hands of the enemy in the Northeast and the righteous soldiers who are resisting the enemy! Sitting and watching the enemy's cavalry advance, and the Yuguan Pass fall! The alarm spread, shaking even Tianjin and Beijing! Such people, compared to rats, cannot help but feel ashamed of themselves!

Alas! If people are not as good as rats, how can they be considered human?

A Shop Assistant's Correspondence: You Can Come, But You Can't Leave 239

Dear Editor:

Last month, a friend from my hometown came to my house, and behind him was a young woman with a large belly. At the time, I thought this must be his new wife. So I congratulated him deeply, on the one hand blaming him for not inviting me to his wedding, and on the other hand congratulating him on the results of their collaboration: a big belly. Unexpectedly, my friend cried, just shook his head and sighed; making me completely confused; later he told me in detail. It turned out that this young woman had been my friend's neighbor since childhood; two years ago she married another man. Because her husband was away all year round, she got involved with my friend: and unexpectedly became pregnant, and could not survive in her hometown. Their original intention in coming to Shanghai was to find some work, but after a month of trying, there was still no way. As for me, it's of course not a problem to take care of them for a month or two; but after a long time, it becomes difficult to continue. They know that I can't take care of them for the rest of their lives, so they want to choose one of the following two paths.

(1) Resolutely return home: but the husband has already filed a lawsuit in court, offering a reward for their arrest; like moths flying into the flame, the situation is really unbearable.

(2) Go their separate ways: my friend, of course, still has a way, but the woman will inevitably commit suicide; to start and then abandon, is against conscience.

Sir: Are there any better ways besides these two? If not, which one is better? Please save them! I wish you

Health, Chen Qikang, respectfully

Editor's note: The new criminal law stipulates that ["A married woman who commits adultery with another person shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than two years, and the adulterer shall be punished in the same way."]. Chen's friend and this woman, of course, deserve what they get; we certainly can't think of any way for him. But on the other hand, a young woman, locked at home keeping a widow's watch, oversteps the boundaries because of sexual frustration; it is really pitiful. ["Spring is too beautiful to keep confined; a branch of red apricot extends over the wall"]; this sentence is really good!

We think that Chen's friend should not abandon this woman under any circumstances; because not only is this an immoral thing, but if she really commits suicide, the legal responsibility will be six or seven times heavier than the simple crime of seduction. Chen can try his best to keep them for a few more days, and try to find a way for them to make a hard living independently, this is the best policy. If it comes to the point where there is no other way, then he can only take the risk and return home resolutely. Fortunately, these kinds of lawsuits at most are only two years; if the judge is particularly lenient, it is hard to say whether they will only be sentenced for two months.

Novel

A Scholarly Family (Continued from 19) 240

— Wang Zhongxian

(10) Loving her is indirectly loving you

Zhongnan questioned Youzhong for a while, and many doubts arose in him. After Youzhong left, there was only Daiqiu in the room. Zhongnan questioned her in a roundabout way, but Daiqiu also remained tight-lipped, refusing to reveal her mother's scandalous behavior. Shinan knew that soft words were ineffective, and suddenly glared his eyes, his face full of murderous intent, and snorted, saying:

["I have already found out that your mother is having an affair as soon as she arrives in Shanghai, what are you still hiding for her? What I don't know is what her lover's name is, you are helping her hide it, I guess you are in collusion with her!"]

Although Zhongnan did not shout loudly, his expression was very stern, and it was somewhat frightening to look at. Daiqiu was already holding a bellyful of grievances that she couldn't express, and she couldn't wait to vent her full belly of complaints. A sentence reached her throat, and she swallowed it down several times with saliva, but she never had the courage to say it. Now seeing this angry face, she was forced to have no choice, she had to... she had to squeeze out a few tears and burst into tears!

. When women encounter urgent matters, they will ask for tears to come to the rescue, especially when dealing with men. No matter how big the matter is, as long as tears are shed, all the difficult problems will be solved.

After Daiqiu left, Zhongnan questioned the maids again, but the result was also fruitless. The time for evening school arrived, and Maosheng came back with a schoolbag. As usual, he had to report to Zhongnan before he could get pocket money to play in the tailor shop. Zhongnan sent the maids away and kept Maosheng by his side, using the interrogation methods of a criminal lawyer to gradually go from shallow to deep, step by step, and trick him into revealing Ruohua's lover. In fact, Maosheng was a very straightforward child, and even if he was asked honestly, he would say it directly and happily. In the tailor shop, he also used Ruohua's anecdotes and scandals with Youzhong as conversation material every day, using this to trick people into giving him spiced beans. Now seeing that his father also loved to listen to this news, he was even more proud, his mouth seemed to have burst a dam, describing his mother's scandalous behavior with his uncle in detail, speaking endlessly. Zhongnan was afraid of interrupting him, so he listened to his animated lecture with a smile. But in his heart, he felt sour and painful, and he couldn't describe the sadness.

Zhongnan got the exact information, gave Maosheng four cents as a reward, and sent him away. He immediately called Lao Hu in and ordered him to invite Fifth Master to talk. Lao Hu went and returned, saying that Fifth Master was not at home and could not be found anywhere. That night, Ruohua returned late after playing. Zhongnan was afraid of the family scandal being spread, so he endured his anger and waited for her to finish her evening makeup. After the maids went to sleep, he called Ruohua closer, stretched out his unfailing hand, gave her a slap first, and then cursed her with gnashing teeth. Ruohua initially wanted to argue, but after Zhongnan presented a few pieces of evidence provided by Maosheng, she bowed her head and said nothing.

Zhongnan warned her: ["Tomorrow, I will invite my old brothers and friends to my house to announce your and Youzhong's crimes, and then publish an announcement in the newspaper to sever brotherly relations with him and to divorce you. We, the Xia family, are a scholarly family passed down from generation to generation, and have never produced such incestuous animals. In order to maintain the etiquette of my family, I will expel this animal from the clan, and I will also report to the government office to expel you this pair of adulterers and adulteresses from the country, and you will never be allowed to come back, lest you harm the local morals!"]

Film Special

On Emil Jannings (Part 1) 241

— Robert Gao

"The Last Command," produced by the German Ufa company, is extraordinary for many reasons. Good material, brilliant direction, beautiful photography, harmonious use of light, proper editing, economical cutting, etc... There is, of course, a tremendous force beyond the success of the performance.

This great world actor, Emil Jannings, is originally a familiar face on our screen. Since 1926 until now, we have seen him many times. He first met us at the Shanghai Grand Theatre before it was renovated. The film he starred in was "Variety." Jannings' internal performance in that play caused all of his muscles to tense up, and his eyes were especially powerful. The clever director called him to perform the whole thing in a calm, natural, deep, and ruthless way, which became his masterpiece of "new edge initially tested."

Jannings' second work was "The Last Laugh," a play with only two subtitles, screened at Carlton. The essence of the play is entirely revealed in his performance, without the help of subtitles, and the audience can fully understand it. It is said that the two subtitles were added only in the United States. From this, we can know the amazingness of Jannings' performance. This is truly a great monument in the world film scene! In "The Last Laugh," he almost performs a solo play, every scene has his actions and expressions, but in every scene, his performance does not seem to be a little slack,

After he performed "The Last Laugh," he was inexplicably hired by the American Paramount Pictures Company. He starred in a total of five films at Paramount, namely "The Way of All Flesh", "The Street of Sin", "The Last Command", "The Patriot", etc. (To be continued)

(1) Review of "Night Nurse" 242

— Ling He

| Carlton Screening |

The political phenomena of each country often consciously reflect new artistic works, and many examples can be found. In this film, for example, the social status of the United States after prohibition, especially the gentlemen and ladies of the upper class who outwardly obey and inwardly disobey this law, is powerfully and humorously exposed. At the same time, their crazy state of wine and beauty is incidentally described, revealing how they are enjoying themselves, and how they are indifferent to their children, thinking that the children are living a beautiful life under the care of nurses hired with money. Therefore, it is not surprising to take baths in milk. Moreover, the treachery and conspiracy of servants in wealthy families are also mentioned.

Under such a theme, the screenwriter is very able to make full use of the technique of lightly touching on the subject. Although some places are slightly lacking in strictness, the whole article is a comedy structure, so it is neither very compact nor very loose, but just a vivid sketch.

Of course, the director put in a lot of effort in this film, and there are many places where his cleverness is revealed. For example, the skeleton and the nurse sleeping in the same bed, although it is a joke, it can be seen its ingenuity. That is, when the head nurse comes in, we all suspect that she will find this skeleton covered by the quilt, but it is not so. The excitement given to the audience is finally intentionally lightly glossed over. It is also not appropriate to simply take off the nurse's clothes to increase the sensuality many times.

Barbara Stanwyck's performance is certainly worthy of appreciation. Her mellow movements and unexaggerated expressions are pleasing. In terms of supporting roles, there are no particularly commendable characters.

The layout is very good, especially the equipment of the rich family, which is enough to write out the comfortable life of the aristocratic woman. The light is soft and beautiful, but not particularly unique, and the pronunciation is clear. However, there is too much dialogue, which is like the taste of a stage play. Although there are many wonderful places, it is definitely not something that the average Chinese person can understand.

(2) A Friend's Wife | Nanjing Screening 243

— God

"A Friend's Wife", Friends Lovers, from the aspect of "name", is already enough to say "good", four famous "name" stars 丨 Adolphe Menjou, Lilian Tashman, Erich von Stroheim and Laurence Harvey 丨 plus an attractive "name", from the aspect of "reality", it has a very dramatic story, clever direction, and clever small actions.

The story seems a little far-fetched, simply narrating that a married young woman is dissatisfied with her husband's temperament, and at the same time unconsciously falls in love with two army officers, colleagues and good friends, who are both British troops stationed in India. They are believers of the three Ws, worshiping war, whiskey, and women, but friendship ultimately triumphs over love. All the actors are very dedicated, fully playing their roles, even the role of the servant, Olgie Hopber, has won our favor.

The director, as mentioned earlier, is very clever. He pays special attention to small actions, like the ending at the British general's mansion, when the two friends met Darte again, Menjou handed the cigarette case to Harvey, and Harvey was stunned and didn't know what to do, all of which are worthy of our praise. The light is very beautiful, and the sound seems to have only ninety-nine percent clarity, perhaps because the machinery in the theater had an occasional malfunction.

Barbara Stanwyck's New Work: Night Nurse 244

— Mu Zhu

Barbara Stanwyck's works are few and far between. Only "Ladies of Leisure" and "Ten Cents a Dance" have been shown in this city. Unfortunately, I read in a magazine that she had fallen and injured her ankle while working in the photography studio at the most tense moment. After being cured by the doctor, she still limps a little when she walks. In this way, her beauty is simply damaged, and she is very annoyed and determined to leave the film industry. Who knew that after a while, she couldn't bear to leave Hollywood, so she returned to the screen. Her most recent work is "Night Nuret", which will soon be screened at Carlton.

German Ufa Company Produces Submarine Films 246

| That is, the German old objects are borrowed from the Finnish government |

Reuter Berlin, 13th. The German Ufa Film Company has recently begun to produce films about the German submarine war. The script requires a "U" submarine, but the German government currently has no submarines. The film company has to borrow a German "U" submarine obtained by Finland after the European War from the Finnish government for application.

Audience Opinions

Discussing "Such a Hero" 247

— Yi Yi

"Such a Hero" can be said to be the first official slapstick film produced domestically, and it has considerable value for attention. I felt satisfied after watching it.

In this film, the directing and set design are not particularly flawed. However, in terms of the plot, there are some shortcomings. Why would the dog owner's child come downstairs at 2:00 AM to release a balloon with a funny face drawn on it? When the thief takes the box, it seems very heavy, as if it's full of things. Why can a child still hide inside later?

Speaking of slapstick films, they originally emphasize action and not facial expressions. In this film, the actions of the two main characters are quite successful, and their facial expressions are not too bad either.

Slapstick films are also very easy to become a chaotic mess. Although the plot of this film is simple, it doesn't become meaningless chaos.

In short, considering that China's film industry is not very developed at present, and this is the first official slapstick film, these results are still good.

The Greatness of "Sign of the Cross" 248

— Yun

丨Cecil B. DeMille's Representative Work丨

Cecil B. DeMille is a director who fully represents the American national character. He often spends thousands upon thousands of gold dollars building ancient city palaces and other sets. At the same time, he spares no expense in hiring a large number of actors to film. He is best at handling those great and well-known historical events. His successful early works are "The Ten Commandments" and "The King of Kings." His most recent miracle is "Sign of the Cross."

The entire performance has extremely unusual power. The actors are all top choices, like Fredric March, Elissa Landi, Claudette Colbert, and Charles Laughton, who is hailed as "the second Emil Jannings." They all give their most outstanding performances.

Originally, the films directed by Cecil B. DeMille are all taken seriously. When filming the bathroom of Poppaea, the extremely extravagant wife of the Roman Emperor Nero, he used a thousand gallons of milk. This is because he researched ancient books and discovered that Poppaea bathed once a day, using the milk of five hundred mules to make "fragrant soup." Not only was this the case in the palace, but when she went to other places, the five hundred mules also accompanied her. For this reason, DeMille specifically went to Southern California to find the cheapest milk. After investigation, he estimated that the price of milk was actually cheaper than the value of artificial milk made by chemical methods, so he resolutely used real milk. At the same time, Claudette Colbert, who played "Poppaea," was also relieved that her skin would not be harmed in the slightest.

After this milk bath was filmed, the remaining one thousand gallons of milk were used as fertilizer for irrigation.

At the same time, the filming time was also delayed due to a particularly heavy costume. The reason is that a costume worn by Poppaea weighed thirty-five pounds. During filming, she was always standing, serving the tyrant Nero. DeMille was afraid that she could not bear the weight, so he specifically allowed Claudette Colbert to work for one hour, rest for fifteen minutes, and then continue working.

The two points mentioned above only appear for a few minutes on the screen, but the filming process took so much time and effort. Here, I dare say that every inch of the film is mixed with DeMille's hard work. Because, in this film, there is not only a great performance, but also a heart-wrenching story of intensified love.

— Xia

Since Wu Suxin left the Great China Company, many companies have wanted her to join them in filming, but she has rejected them all. Besides filming at Huimin Company, which was founded by her husband Zhang Huimin, she spends her days at home with the radio on. Recently, she has hired a scholar in a blue gown to study Peking Opera. She once belonged to a troupe, so she is able to perform more than twenty operas.

Li Lili, the "Sweet Girl" of the Bright Moon Dance Troupe, will soon perform a modern drama donated by Shanghai at the Beijing Grand Theater.

Film Novel Deserted Wife BiuofDivorceinent (16) 250

Hilary knew that his Ma had gone with Gray, and he stopped pretending and returned to his original state. "Good, dear Shirley, I am now a lonely child."

She looked at him, surprised at his composure. He didn't seem crazy at all. How could he be so calm? Yes, he was pretending to be crazy! Tears welled up in her eyes. "Father, you sacrificed yourself, leaving them! Ah, you must love her so much! But you won't be alone—I'm here."

Hilary stood up and walked towards her. What about Cade? "What about your marriage?"

"It's all settled, Father. We are in the same boat, sharing the same fate. We should stay together." He was extremely moved and stretched out his arms, holding her tightly. "My poor, dear child. I have ruined your life. But I will give you a new life. I will make you happy—we will enjoy ourselves together. You wait and see."

As he was speaking, Shirley heard Cade's long, clear sigh. She shuddered for a moment and walked to the window, but she only pulled down the curtains. "I can't, dear Cade," she whispered. "I can't go with you. May God bless you."

She returned to Hilary's side. "Father, let's play your Sonata together. Do you remember? ... It's so moving!"

They sat by the piano, obeying the fortunate arrangement that bound them together. Shirley's heart was shattered, but she was determined to continue her sacrifice—to maintain her father's happiness, no matter the cost. (The End)
